        nārīlocanacāturyaśaṅkāsaṃkucitaṃya thā //599//}	nArI locana cAturya SaFkA saMkucitaMya TAH //599//}
                       (Śrivatsalāñchanācārya's Kāvyaparīkṣā 340)	(Śrivatsa lAQCana AcArya as KAvya parIkzA 340)
   utprekṣitamapi tāttvikena rūpeṇa parivarjitatvāt nirupākhyaprakhyam /	utprekzitam api tAttvikena rUpeNa parivarjita tvAt nirupAKya praKyam /
   tatsamarthanāya yat arthāntaranyāsopādānam tat ālekhyamiva	tad samarTanAya yat arTa antaranyAsa upAdAnam tat AleKyam iva
   gaganataletyantamasamīcīnamiti nirviṣayatvametasya / anucitārthataiva	gagana talA iti antam asamIcInam iti nirvizaya tvam etasya / anucita arTa tA eva
   doṣaḥ / yathā	dozaH / yaTA
        {divākarādrakṣati yo guhāsu līnaṃ divā bhītamivāndhakāram /	{divAkarAt rakzati yaH guhAsu lInam divA BItam iva anDakAram /
        kṣudre 'pi nūnaṃ prapanne mamatvamuccaiḥ śirasāmatīva //600//}	kzudre api nUnam prapanne mamatvam uccEs SirasAm atIva //600//}
                       (Kālidāsa's Kumārasaṃbhava 1.12)	(KAli dAsa as KumAra saMBavaH 1.12)
   atrācetanasya tamaso divākarāttrāsa eva na saṃbhavatīti kuta eva	atra acetanasya tamasaH divAkarAt trAsaH eva na saMBavati iti kutas eva
   tatprayojitamadriṇā paritrāṇam / saṃbhāvitena tu rūpeṇa	tad prayojitam adriNA paritrANam / saMBAvitena tu rUpeNa
   pratibhāsamānasyāsya na kācidanupapattiravataratīti vyartha eva	pratiBAsamAnasya asya na kAcid anupapattiH avatarati iti vyarTaH eva
   tatsamarthanāyāṃ yatnaḥ /	tad samarTanAyAm yatnaH /
   sādhāraṇaviśeṣaṇavaśādeva samāsoktiranuktamapi upamānaviśeṣaṃ	sADAraNa viSezaNa vaSAt eva samAsa uktiH anuktam api upamAna viSezam
   prakāśayatīti tasyātra punarupādāne prayojanābhāvāt anupādeyatvaṃ yat tat	prakASayati iti tasya atra punar upAdAne prayojana aBAvAt anupAdeya tvam yat tat 
   apuṣṭārthatvaṃ punaruktaṃ vā doṣaḥ / yathā	apuzwa arTa tvam punaruktam vA dozaH / yaTA
        {spṛśati tigmarucau kakubhaḥ karairdayitayeva vijṛmbhitatāpayā /	{spRSati tigma rucO kakuBaH karEH dayitayA iva vijRmBita tApayA /
        atanumānaparigrahayā sthitaṃ rucirayā cirayāpi dinaśriyā //601//}	atanu mAna parigrahayA sTitam rucirayA cirayA api dina SriyA //601//}
                       (Ratnākara's Haravijaya 3.37)	(RatnAkara as HaravijayaH 3.37)
   atra tigmaruceḥ kakubhāṃ ca yathā sadṛśaviśeṣaṇavaśena	atra tigma ruceH kakuBAm ca yaTA sadRSa viSezaNa vaSena
   vyaktiviśeṣaparigraheṇa ca nāyakatayā nāyikātvena ca vyaktiḥ, tathā	vyakti viSeza parigraheNa ca nAyaka tayA nAyikA tvena ca vyaktiH, taTA
   grīṣmadivasaśriyo 'pi pratināyikātvena bhaviṣyatīti kiṃ dayitayeti	grIzma divasa SriyaH api pratinAyikA tvena Bavizyati iti kim dayitayA iti
   svaśabdopādānena //	sva Sabda upAdAnena //
   śleṣopamāyāstu sa viṣayaḥ yatropamānasyopādānamantareṇa sādhāraṇeṣvapi	Sleza upamAyAH tu sa vizayaH yatra upamAnasya upAdAnam antareNa sADAraNezu api
   viśeṣaṇeṣu na tathā pratītiḥ / yathā	viSezaNezu na taTA pratItiH / yaTA
        {svayaṃ ca pallavātāmra bhāsvatkaravirājitā /	{svayam ca pallavAH tAmra BAsvat karavirAjitA /
        prabhātasaṃdhyevāsvāpaphalalubdhehitapradā //602//} iti//	praBAta saMDyA iva AsvApa Pala lubDa Ihita pradA //602//} iti//
                       (Udbhaṭa's Kāvyālaṅkārasārasaṅgraha 4.15)	(u udBawa as KAvya alaFkAra sAra saFgrahaH 4.15)
   aprastutapraśaṃsāyāmapi upameyam anayaiva rītyā pratītaṃ na punaḥ	aprastuta praSaMsAyAm api upameyam anayA eva rItyA pratItam na punar 
   prayogeṇa kadarthatāṃ neyam / yathā	prayogeNa kadarTa tAm na iyam / yaTA
        {āhūteṣu vihaṅgameṣu maśako nāyān puro vāryate	{a AhUtezu vihaFgamezu maSakaH na ayAn puras vAryate
             madhyevāridhi vāvasaṃstṛṇamaṇirdhatte maṇīnāṃ rucam /	maDyevAriDi vA avasan= tRNa maNiH Datte maNInAm rucam /
        khadyoto 'pi na kampate pracalituṃ madhye 'pi tejasvināṃ	KadyotaH api na kampate pracalitum maDye api tejasvinAm
             dhik sāmānyamacetanaṃ prabhumivānāmṛṣṭatattvāntaram //603//}	Dik sAmAnyam acetanam praBum iva anAmRzwa tattva antaram //603//}
                       (Bhallaṭaśataka 67)	(Bhat lawa SatakaH 67)
   atra acetanasya prabhoraprastutaviśiṣṭasāmānyadvāreṇābhivyaktau na	atra acetanasya praBoH aprastuta viSizwa sAmAnya dvAreNa aBivyaktO na
   yuktameva punaḥ kathanam //	yuktam eva punar kaTanam //
   tadeta alaṅkāradoṣāḥ yathāsaṃbhāvinonye 'pyevañjātīyakāḥ pūrvoktayaiva	tadA Ita alaFkAra dozAH yaTA saMBAvinonye api evan jAtIyakAH pUrva uktayA eva
   doṣajātyā antarbhāvitāḥ na pṛthag pratipādanamarhantīti saṃpūrṇamidaṃ	doza jAtyAH antar BAvitAH na pRTak pratipAdanam arhanti iti saMpUrNam idam
   kāvyalakṣaṇam //142//	kAvya lakzaNam //142//
        {ityeṣa mārgo viduṣāṃ vibhinno 'pyabhinnarūpaḥ pratibhāsate yat /	{iti eza mArgaH viduzAm viBinnaH api aBinna rUpaH pratiBAsate yat /
        na tadvicitraṃ yadamutra samyagvinirmitā saṃghaṭanaiva hetuḥ //1//}	na tad vicitram yat amutra samyak vinirmitA saMGawana eva hetuH //1//}
   iti kāvyaprakāśe 'rthālaṅkāranirṇayo nāma daśama ullāsaḥ //	iti kAvya prakASe arTAlaFkAra nirNayaH nAma daSame ullAsaH //
